(declare-fun i_loop () (_ BitVec 17))
(declare-fun i-loop () Int)
(assert (and (> i-loop 0) (< i-loop 16)))
(assert (= ((_ int2bv 17) i-loop) i_loop))
(define-fun getbit ((x (_ BitVec 17)) (index (_ BitVec 17))) (_ BitVec 1)
	((_ extract 0 0) (bvlshr x index)))

(define-fun loopConV ((x (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(and
		(= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 16 16) x)) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop
		(= (getbit (bvshl x (_ bv1 17)) i_loop) ((_ extract 15 15) x)))) ;; k ~ i_loop-1

(define-fun loopConF ((x (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 16 16) x))) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop

(define-fun next ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
    (and
    	(= ((_ extract 15 0) fap) ((_ extract 16 1) A))
		(loopConF fap)))
		
(define-fun yesterday ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
    (= fap (bvshl A (_ bv1 17))))
		
(define-fun zeta ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
    (= fap (bvor (bvshl A (_ bv1 17)) (_ bv1 17))))

(define-fun until ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17)) (B (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(and
		(= ((_ extract 15 0) fap) (bvor ((_ extract 15 0) B) (bvand ((_ extract 15 0) A) ((_ extract 16 1) fap))))
		(= #b1 (bvor ((_ extract 16 16) A) ((_ extract 16 16) B) (bvnot ((_ extract 16 16) fap))))
		(= #b1 (bvor (bvnot ((_ extract 16 16) B)) ((_ extract 16 16) fap)))
		(loopConF fap)
		(or (= #b0 ((_ extract 16 16) fap))
			(bvugt B (bvshl (_ bv1 17) i_loop)))))

(define-fun release ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17)) (B (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(until (bvnot fap) (bvnot A) (bvnot B)))

(define-fun since ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17)) (B (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(and
		(= ((_ extract 0 0) fap) ((_ extract 0 0) B) )
		(= ((_ extract 16 1) fap) (bvor ((_ extract 16 1) B) (bvand ((_ extract 16 1) A) ((_ extract 15 0) fap))))))

(define-fun trigger ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17)) (B (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(since (bvnot fap) (bvnot A) (bvnot B)))

(define-fun alw ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(= fap ((_ repeat 17) (bvredand A))))

(define-fun som ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(= fap ((_ repeat 17) (bvredor A))))

(define-fun alwf ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(until (bvnot fap) #b11111111111111111 (bvnot A)))

(define-fun alwp ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
    (since (bvnot fap) #b11111111111111111 (bvnot A)))

(define-fun somp ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
    (since fap #b11111111111111111 A))

(define-fun somf ((fap (_ BitVec 17)) (A (_ BitVec 17))) Bool
	(until fap #b11111111111111111 A))

(define-fun bviff ((A (_ BitVec 17)) (B (_ BitVec 17))) (_ BitVec 17)
    (bvxnor A B))
